\"public\".\"generate_event_slug\"(\"event_title\" \"text\") RETURNS \"text\"\n    LANGUAGE \"plpgsql\"\n    AS 
$$\nDECLARE\n    base_slug text;\n    final_slug text;\n    counter integer := 0;\nBEGIN\n    -- Convert title to slug 
format\n    base_slug := lower(regexp_replace(event_title, '[^a-zA-Z0-9\\s]', '', 'g'));\n    base_slug := 
regexp_replace(base_slug, '\\s+', '-', 'g');\n    base_slug := trim(both '-' from base_slug);\n    \n    final_slug := 
base_slug;\n    \n    -- Check if slug exists and increment counter if needed\n    WHILE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM 
public.events WHERE slug = final_slug) LOOP\n        counter := counter + 1;\n        final_slug := base_slug || '-' 
|| counter;\n    END LOOP;\n    \n    RETURN final_slug;\nEND;\n$$","ParameterOIDs":null}

\"public\".\"get_event_analytics\"(\"user_uuid\" \"uuid\" DEFAULT NULL::\"uuid\") RETURNS TABLE(\"total_events\" 
bigint, \"upcoming_events\" bigint, \"ongoing_events\" bigint, \"completed_events\" bigint, \"cancelled_events\" 
bigint, \"total_capacity\" bigint, \"events_this_month\" bigint, \"events_this_week\" bigint, 
\"most_popular_category\" \"text\", \"average_capacity\" numeric)\n    LANGUAGE \"plpgsql\" SECURITY DEFINER\n    AS 
$$\nBEGIN\n    RETURN QUERY\n    WITH event_stats AS (\n        SELECT \n            COUNT(*) as total,\n            
COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'upcoming') as upcoming,\n            COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'ongoing') as 
ongoing,\n            COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE status = 'completed') as completed,\n            COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE 
status = 'cancelled') as cancelled,\n            COALESCE(SUM(capacity), 0) as total_cap,\n            COUNT(*) FILTER 
(WHERE DATE_TRUNC('month', created_at) = DATE_TRUNC('month', CURRENT_DATE)) as month_count,\n            COUNT(*) 
FILTER (WHERE created_at \u003e= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '7 days') as week_count,\n            AVG(capacity) as 
avg_cap\n        FROM public.events e\n        WHERE (user_uuid IS NULL OR e.user_id = user_uuid)\n    ),\n    
popular_category AS (\n        SELECT category\n        FROM public.events e\n        WHERE (user_uuid IS NULL OR 
e.user_id = user_uuid)\n        GROUP BY category\n        ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC\n        LIMIT 1\n    )\n    SELECT 
\n        es.total,\n        es.upcoming,\n        es.ongoing,\n        es.completed,\n        es.cancelled,\n        
es.total_cap,\n        es.month_count,\n        es.week_count,\n        COALESCE(pc.category, 'N/A'),\n        
ROUND(es.avg_cap, 2)\n    FROM event_stats es\n    CROSS JOIN popular_category pc;\nEND;\n$$","ParameterOIDs":null}
